<p>娉锛璇ラㄥ<code>&lt;typename&gt;</code>绫诲锛浠ユ虹绫诲锛ゅ<code>void</code>锛涔浠ユ绫汇<code>&lt;identifier&gt;</code>璇绗</p>
<p>扮涓绉浠ュㄦ寤虹寮ㄧ被锛垮害涓瑕ㄥ０跺纭瀹</p>
<p>澹版璇ョ璇娉瑕姹涓<code>&lt;typename&gt;[] &lt;identifier&gt;(=&lt;initial sentence&gt;);</code></p>
<p>渚濡锛<code>bool[] flag;</code> 涓ュ娉澹版璇ワ涓寤虹扮ㄥ寤哄瀵瑰间负<code>null</code>锛姝ゆ惰块扮涓瀹涔</p>
<p><strong>姝ゅ娉ㄦ哄浼缁C++澹版扮瑰锛浠ㄧJava澹版瑰</strong></p>
<p>寤烘扮浠ョnew抽瀛寤恒</p>
<p>寤烘扮璇ヨ娉瑕姹<code>(&lt;typename&gt;[]) &lt;identifier&gt; = new &lt;typename&gt;[arraySize];</code></p>
<p>渚濡锛<code>flag = new bool[10];</code> 涓绉娉寤烘瑰寤烘扮蹇椤诲跺扮垮害锛规蜂腑浠浠ヤヤ涓村般扮垮害涓瀹灏浜$2^{31}-1$</p>
<p>ㄦ浠Mx*涓锛扮涓芥杩ㄦ寤虹寤烘扮锛褰㈠锛<code>&lt;typename&gt;[] &lt;identifier&gt;[arraySize]</code>瀹涔扮锛榛璁ゅ兼Null锛姝ゆ朵娇ㄦ扮涓璁块绱瀹涔</p>
<p><strong>扮寤烘规</strong>锛<code>&lt;identifier&gt;.size()</code>杩扮垮害锛芥拌间负<code>int</code>瀵<code>null</code>扮瀵硅薄ц<code>.size()</code>杩扮垮害瀹涔</p>
<p><strong>澶缁存扮</strong>锛浠ㄤ氦扮ヨ揪板缁存扮锛浜ら扮灏辨扮扮澹版规C#璇瑷淇涓达浠ョ瑙ｄ负C++璇瑷涓vector濂vector</p>
<p>澹版浜ら扮璇ヨ娉瑕姹涓<code>&lt;typename&gt;[]... &lt;identifier&gt;(=&lt;initial sentence&gt;);</code></p>
<p>渚濡澹版涓涓2缁存扮璇ュ浠ユ锛<code>int[][] graph;</code></p>
<p>澹版<strong>寤</strong>浜ら扮璇娉涓猴<code>(&lt;typename&gt;[]...) &lt;identifier&gt; = new &lt;typename&gt;[outerSize][]..;</code></p>
<p>寤轰氦扮瑕寤烘澶灞扮绌洪达跺寤哄灞扮绌洪淬绫讳技浜C++std::vector</p>
<p>渚濡澹版寤轰涓2缁存扮璇ュ浠ユ锛</p>

<h4><a id="user-content-93-芥拌" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#93-芥拌"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a><strong>9.3 芥拌</strong></h4>
<p>濡芥板０杩间<code>void</code>锛搴<code>return</code>璇ヨ芥拌硷涔瀹涔锛渚澶锛<code>main</code>芥颁澶锛浠ユ病杩硷姝ゆ惰间负0锛</p>
<p>濡芥板０杩兼<code>void</code>锛<code>return</code>璇ュ蹇椤诲虹拌〃绀轰姝や缃璺冲哄芥帮<code>return;</code>锛锛涔璇娉璇璇ヨ娉璇涓鸿间负<code>void</code>芥板藉浣跨锛<code>return;</code>锛浠讳<code>return &lt;expr&gt;;</code>涓鸿娉璇</p>
<p>Semantic Check舵碉杩绫诲<code>void</code>杩奸瑕妫ュ芥颁腑姣涓涓<code>return</code>璇ョ杩绫诲姝ｇ‘锛浣涓鸿娉妫ャ</p>
<p>杩煎浠ユ瀹涔绫伙浠ユ扮锛浠ユ瀹涔绫荤扮瀵逛扮绫诲杩奸瑕妫ョ淮版姝ｇ‘锛涔灏辨2缁存扮涓浠ヨ缁1缁存扮锛淇璇缁村害涓垮害涓瀹归</p>
<p>渚濡锛浠ヤ典浼虹板ㄦ璇逛腑锛</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c++ position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="int[] foo(int args){
  return new int[args];
}

int main(){
  int[] vec = foo(10);
  return vec[11]; // Out-of-range Exception.
}
"><pre><span class="pl-k">int</span>[] foo(<span class="pl-k">int</span> args){
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-k">int</span>[args];
}

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>(){
  <span class="pl-k">int</span>[] vec = <span class="pl-c1">foo</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>);

<h4><a id="user-content-94-lambda-琛ㄨ揪寮" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#94-lambda-琛ㄨ揪寮"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a><strong>9.4 Lambda 琛ㄨ揪寮锛</strong></h4>
<p>Lambda琛ㄨ揪寮宸茬涓虹颁唬绋搴璇瑷涓甯搁瑕涓涓斤瀹浠ョ浠ｇ渚濡濡涓涓ょ浠ｇ绛</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-java position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Arrays.sort(array, new Comparator&lt;String&gt;() {
    public int compare(String s1, String s2) {
        return s1.compareTo(s2);
    }
});
"><pre><span class="pl-smi">Arrays</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>sort(array, <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-k">Comparator&lt;<span class="pl-smi">String</span>&gt;</span>() {
